<div>&lt;p&gt;Choose the situation that is closest to what you are experiencing,  and we will take you through the problem-solving process step-by-step.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;This document explains the process of upgrading a 32-bit agent to a 64-bit agent, considering the prerequisites and dependencies.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following error message is displayed when taking a backup:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Unable to delete &amp;lt;file&amp;gt; or unable to move &amp;lt;file&amp;gt; because it is used by another process.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;This issue normally occurs for any cache files/log files.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To resolve this issue, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Check if there were any tasks running when the  agent was killed.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to the file path specified in the  error message and attempt to delete it only if it is a Log file or a cache  file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If memory errors occur, clear up some space to have enough space to backup the &lt;em&gt;main&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;directory.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#77114350-3ae5-11e5-913f-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#519fc300-3ae3-11e5-b29d-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back77114350-3ae5-11e5-913f-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#519fc300-3ae3-11e5-b29d-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following error message is displayed when taking a backup:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Unable to delete &amp;lt;file&amp;gt; or unable to move &amp;lt;file&amp;gt; because it is used by another process.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;This issue normally occurs for any cache files/log files.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To resolve this issue, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Check if there were any tasks running when the  agent was killed.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to the file path specified in the  error message and attempt to delete it only if it is a Log file or a cache  file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Once the installation completes, the agent needs to be started by running the command:&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;infaagent startup&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;G&lt;/em&gt;o to&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;SecureAgent_InstallDirectory&amp;gt;/main/agentcore and &lt;/em&gt;run the following command: &lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;consoleAgentManager.sh getstatus&lt;br /&gt; &lt;/em&gt;This should return&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Not_configured confirming that the agent is running but is not configured.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the agent to register it to your organization by running command: &lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;consoleAgentManager.sh configure &amp;lt;username&amp;gt; &amp;lt;password&amp;gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Setup proxy if applicable.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;SAP: Follow the user guide and setup the SAP 64 bit libraries on the agent.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Custom patches: Apply all the custom patches if available at appropriate locations.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to the file path specified in the error message and attempt to delete it only if it is a Log file or a cache file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to the file path specified in the error message and attempt to delete it only if it is a Log file or a cache file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To resolve this issue, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Setup proxy if applicable.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Choose to run as a log on user if needed: Go to &lt;em&gt;Logon&lt;/em&gt; tab in the &lt;em&gt;Properties&lt;/em&gt; menu of the Informatica Cloud secure agent service.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;SAP: Follow the user guide and setup the SAP 64-bit libraries on the agent.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Custom patches: Apply all the custom patches if available at appropriate locations.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
